<h1 _ngcontent-vle-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="TextInput"> TextInput </h1>

<div _ngcontent-vle-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>单行文本输入框组件。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>该组件从API version 7开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>      <p>该组件仅支持单文本样式，若需实现富文本样式，建议使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-richeditor">RichEditor</a>组件。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>无</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 429px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>TextInput(value?: TextInputOptions)</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#textinputoptions对象说明">TextInputOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">TextInput组件参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 831px;">     <h2 id="textinputoptions对象说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">TextInputOptions对象说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textinputoptions对象说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>TextInput初始化参数。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.5.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">placeholder</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">设置无输入时的提示文本。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">text</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>设置输入框当前的文本内容。</p>          <p>建议通过onChange事件将状态变量与文本实时绑定，</p>          <p>避免组件刷新时TextInput中的文本内容异常。</p>          <p>从API version 10开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-two-way-sync" target="_blank">$$</a>双向绑定变量。</p>          <p>从API version 18开始，该参数支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-new-binding#系统组件参数双向绑定" target="_blank">!!</a>双向绑定变量。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">controller<sup>8+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#textinputcontroller8">TextInputController</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">设置TextInput控制器。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 682px;">     <h2 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>除支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-component-general-attributes">通用属性</a>，还支持以下属性：</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>默认情况下，通用属性<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#padding">padding</a>的默认值为：</p>       <p>{</p>       <p>top: '8vp',</p>       <p>right: '16vp',</p>       <p>bottom: '8vp',</p>       <p>left: '16vp'</p>       <p>}</p>       <p>输入框开启下划线模式时，通用属性padding的默认值为：</p>       <p>{</p>       <p>top: '12vp',</p>       <p>right: '0vp',</p>       <p>bottom: '12vp',</p>       <p>left: '0vp'</p>       <p>}</p>       <p>当输入框设置padding为0时，可设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-border#borderradius">borderRadius</a>为0避免光标被截断。当光标在文本框边缘显示异常时，请检查是否是padding、borderRadius属性影响造成。</p>       <p>从API version 10开始，单行输入框可设置.width('auto')使组件宽度自适应文本宽度，自适应时组件宽度受constraintSize属性以及父容器传递的最大最小宽度限制，其余使用方式参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size">尺寸设置</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 641px;">     <h3 id="type" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">type<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="type" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type(value: InputType)</p>     <p>设置输入框类型。</p>     <p>不同的InputType会拉起对应类型的键盘，同时限制输入。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#inputtype枚举说明">InputType</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>输入框类型。</p>          <p>默认值：InputType.Normal</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>密码填充服务需要特定的输入框类型。如何使用密码填充服务参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/passwordvault-quick-adaptation" target="_blank">快速适配</a>。</p>       <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#密码模式" target="_blank">密码模式</a>时，装饰线<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#decoration12">decoration</a>、下划线<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#showunderline10">showUnderline</a>不生效。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 541px;">     <h3 id="placeholdercolor" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">placeholderColor<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="placeholdercolor" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span auto 661px;">     <h3 id="maxlength" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">maxLength<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="maxlength" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 634px;">     <h3 id="inputfilter8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputFilter<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="inputfilter8" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>inputFilter(value: ResourceStr, error?: Callback&lt;string&gt;)</p>     <p>通过正则表达式设置输入过滤器。匹配表达式的输入允许显示，不匹配的输入将被过滤。</p>     <p>单字符输入场景仅支持单字符匹配，多字符输入场景支持字符串匹配，例如粘贴。</p>     <p>从API version 11开始，设置inputFilter且输入的字符不为空字符，会导致<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#type">type</a>接口附带的文本过滤效果失效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textcontentstyle10">TextContentStyle</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>输入框为默认风格或内联输入风格。</p>          <p>默认值：TextInputStyle.Default</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 817px;">     <h3 id="textalign9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textAlign<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textalign9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textAlign(value: TextAlign)</p>     <p>设置文本在输入框中的水平对齐方式。</p>     <p>支持TextAlign.Start、TextAlign.Center和TextAlign.End。TextAlign.JUSTIFY的对齐方式按照TextAlign.Start处理。</p>     <p>可通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-location#align">align</a>属性控制文本段落在垂直方向上的位置。此组件中不可使用align属性控制文本段落在水平方向上的位置。</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>Alignment.TopStart、Alignment.Top、Alignment.TopEnd：内容顶部对齐。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Alignment.Start、Alignment.Center、Alignment.End：内容垂直居中。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Alignment.BottomStart、Alignment.Bottom、Alignment.BottomEnd：内容底部对齐。</p></li>     </ul>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textalign">TextAlign</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本在输入框中的水平对齐方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextAlign.Start</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>textAlign只能调整文本整体的布局，不影响字符的显示顺序。若需要调整字符的显示顺序，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-internationalization#镜像状态字符对齐" target="_blank">镜像状态字符对齐</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div  <h3 id="showerror10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">showError<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon <p>当参数类型为ResourceStr并且输入内容不符合定义规范时，提示错误文本，当提示错误单行文本超长时，末尾以省略号显示。当参数类型为undefined时，不显示错误状态。请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#示例2设置下划线">示例2</a>。</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">customKeyboard<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="customkeyboard10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>customKeyboard(value: CustomBuilder, options?: KeyboardOptions)</p>     <p>设置自定义键盘。</p>     <p>当设置自定义键盘时，输入框激活后不会打开系统输入法，而是加载指定的自定义组件。</p>     <p>自定义键盘的高度可以通过自定义组件根节点的height属性设置，宽度不可设置，使用系统默认值。</p>     <p>自定义键盘采用覆盖原始界面的方式呈现，当没有开启避让模式或者输入框不需要避让的场景不会对应用原始界面产生压缩或者上提。</p>     <p>自定义键盘无法获取焦点，但是会拦截手势事件。</p>     <p>默认在输入控件失去焦点时，关闭自定义键盘，开发者也可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#textinputcontroller8">TextInputController</a>.<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#stopediting10">stopEditing</a>方法控制键盘关闭。</p>     <p>当设置自定义键盘时，可以通过绑定<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-events-key#onkeypreime12">onKeyPrelme</a>事件规避物理键盘的输入。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.14.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.34.14.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>自定义键盘。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>showCounter(value: boolean, options?: InputCounterOptions)</p>     <p>设置当通过InputCounterOptions输入的字符数超过阈值时显示计数器。未调用showCounter接口时，默认不显示计数器。</p>     <p>参数value为true时，才能设置options，文本框开启计数下标功能，需要配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#maxlength">maxLength</a>（设置最大字符限制）一起使用。字符计数器显示的效果是当前输入字符数/最大可输入字符数。</p>     <p>当输入字符数大于最大字符数乘百分比值时，显示字符计数器。如果用户设置计数器时不设置InputCounterOptions，那么当前输入字符数超过最大字符数时，边框和计数器下标将变为红色。用户同时设置参数value为true和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-text-style#inputcounteroptions11对象说明">InputCounterOptions</a>，当thresholdPercentage数值在有效区间内，且输入字符数超过最大字符数时，边框和计数器下标将变为红色，框体抖动。highlightBorder设置为false，则不显示红色边框，计数器默认显示红色，框体抖动。</p>     <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#内联模式" target="_blank">内联模式</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#密码模式" target="_blank">密码模式</a>下字符计数器不显示。</p>     <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#示例5设置计数器">示例5（设置计数器）</a>展示了设置showCounter的效果。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 12开始，该接口支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否显示计数器。</p>          <p>true表示显示计数器，false表示不显示。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">计数器的配置项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">underlineColor<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <h3 id="lineheight12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">lineHeight<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon <p>设置值不大于0时，不限制文本行高，自适应字体大小，number类型时单位为fp。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a width="25%">文本的文本行高。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>特殊字符字体高度远超出同行的其他字符高度时，文本框出现截断、遮挡、内容相对位置发生变化等不符合预期的显示异常，需要开发者调整组件高度、行高等属性，修改对应的页面布局。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 825px;">     <h3 id="decoration12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">decoration<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="decoration12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>decoration(value: TextDecorationOptions)</p>     <p>设置文本装饰线类型样式及其颜色。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.43.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead> width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本装饰线对象。</p>          <p>默认值：{</p>          <p>type: TextDecorationType.None,</p>          <p>color: Color.Black,</p>          <p>style: TextDecorationStyle.SOLID</p>          <p>}</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当文字的下边缘轮廓与装饰线位置相交时，会触发下划线避让规则，下划线将在这些字符处避让文字。常见“gjyqp”等英文字符。</p>       <p>当文本装饰线的颜色设置为Color.Transparent时，装饰线颜色设置为跟随每行第一个字的字体颜色。当文本装饰线的颜色设置为透明色16进制对应值“#00FFFFFF”时，装饰线颜色设置为透明色。</p>       <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#密码模式" target="_blank">密码模式</a>时，装饰线<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#decoration12">decoration</a>、下划线<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#showunderline10">showUnderline</a>不生效。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="letterspacing12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">letterSpacing<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="letterspacing12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>letterSpacing(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本字符间距。设置该值为百分比时，按默认值显示。设置该值为0时，按默认值显示。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>当取值为负值时，文字会发生压缩，负值过小时会将组件内容区大小压缩为0，导致无内容显示。</p>     <p>对每个字符生效，包括行尾字符。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> id="mcps1.3.44.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource">Resource</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本字符间距。</p>          <p>单位：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-pixel-units">fp</a></p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 945px;">     <h3 id="fontfeature12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontFeature<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fontfeature12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fontFeature(value: string)</p>     <p>设置文字特性效果，比如数字等宽的特性。</p>     <p>格式为：normal | &lt;feature-tag-value&gt;</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的格式为：&lt;string&gt; [ &lt;integer&gt; | on | off ]</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的个数可以有多个，中间用','隔开。</p>     <p>例如，使用等宽数字的输入格式为："ss01" on。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.11.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文字特性效果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>Font Feature当前支持的属性见 <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#fontfeature12">fontFeature属性列表</a>。</p>     <p>设置 Font Feature 属性，Font Feature 是 OpenType 字体的高级排版能力，如支持连字、数字等宽等特性，一般用在自定义字体中，其能力需要字体本身支持。</p>     <p>更多 Font Feature 能力介绍可参考 <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop" target="_blank">https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop</a> 和 <a href="https://sparanoid.com/lab/opentype-features/" target="_blank">https://sparanoid.com/lab/opentype-features/</a></p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#密码模式" target="_blank">密码模式</a>时，不支持通过fontFeature设置文本样式。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 633px;">     <h3 id="wordbreak12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wordBreak<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wordbreak12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>wordBreak(value: WordBreak)</p>     <p>设置文本断行规则。该属性在组件设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#内联模式" target="_blank">内联模式</a>时样式生效，但对placeholder文本无效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.7.1.5.1.2" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>内联输入风格编辑态时断行规则。</p>          <p>默认值：WordBreak.BREAK_WORD</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>组件不支持clip属性设置，设置该属性任意枚举值对组件文本截断无影响。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 825px;">     <h3 id="textoverflow12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textOverflow<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textoverflow12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textOverflow(value: TextOverflow)</p>     <p>设置文本超长时的显示方式。仅在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#内联模式" target="_blank">内联模式</a>的编辑态、非编辑态下支持。</p>     <p>文本截断是按字进行。例如，英文以单词为最小单位进行截断，若需要以字母为单位进行截断，可将wordBreak属性设置为WordBreak.BREAK_ALL。</p>     <p>当overflow设置为TextOverflow.None时，效果与TextOverflow.Clip相同。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>TextInput组件不支持设置TextOverflow.MARQUEE模式，当设置为TextOverflow.MARQUEE模式时，<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#内联模式" target="_blank">内联模式</a>非编辑态下显示为TextOverflow.Ellipsis，内联模式编辑态下以及非内联模式下显示为TextOverflow.Clip。</p>       <p>未设置内联模式时，按照默认风格显示。若此时设置textOverflow，则不生效。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="textindent12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textIndent<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a 637px;">     <h3 id="minfontsize12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">minFontSize<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="minfontsize12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>minFontSize(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本最小显示字号。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#maxfontsize12">maxFontSize</a>以及<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#maxlines10">maxLines</a>(组件设置为内联输入风格且编辑态时使用)或布局大小限制使用，单独设置不生效。</p>     <p>自适应字号生效时，fontSize设置不生效。</p>     <p>minFontSize小于或等于0时，自适应字号不生效，此时按照<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#fontsize">fontSize</a>属性的值生效，未设置时按照其默认值生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 661px;">     <h3 id="maxfontsize12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">maxFontSize<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>maxFontSize(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本最大显示字号。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#minfontsize12">minFontSize</a>以及<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#maxlines10">maxLines</a>(组件设置为内联输入风格且编辑态时使用)或布局大小限制使用，单独设置不生效。</p>     <p>自适应字号生效时，fontSize设置不生效。</p>     <p>maxFontSize小于等于0或者maxFontSize小于minFontSize时，自适应字号不生效，此时按照<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#fontsize">fontSize</a>属性的值生效，未设置时按照其默认值生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"   <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本最大显示字号。</p>          <p>单位：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-pixel-units">fp</a></p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 921px;">     <h3 id="heightadaptivepolicy12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">heightAdaptivePolicy<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="heightadaptivepolicy12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>heightAdaptivePolicy(value: TextHeightAdaptivePolicy)</p>     <p>组件设置为内联输入风格时，设置文本自适应高度的方式。</p>     <p>当设置为TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MAX_LINES_FIRST时，优先使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#maxlines10">maxLines</a>属性来调整文本高度。如果使用maxLines属性的布局大小超过了布局约束，则尝试在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#minfontsize12">minFontSize</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#maxfontsize12">maxFontSize</a>的范围内缩小字体以显示更多文本。</p>     <p>当设置为TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MIN_FONT_SIZE_FIRST时，优先使用minFontSize属性来调整文本高度。如果使用minFontSize属性可以将文本布局在一行中，则尝试在minFontSize和maxFontSize的范围内增大字体并使用最大可能的字体大小。</p>     <p>当设置为TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.LAYOUT_CONSTRAINT_FIRST时，与TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MIN_FONT_SIZE_FIRST效果一样。</p>     <p>组件设置为非内联输入风格时，设置文本自适应高度(TextHeightAdaptivePolicy)的三种方式效果一样，即在minFontSize和maxFontSize的范围内缩小字体以显示更多文本。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>组件设置为内联输入风格，编辑态与非编辑态存在字体大小不一致情况。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textheightadaptivepolicy10">TextHeightAdaptivePolicy</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本自适应高度的方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MAX_LINES_FIRST</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 685px;">     <h3 id="showpassword12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">showPassword<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="showpassword12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>showPassword(visible: boolean)</p>     <p>设置密码的显隐状态。</p>     <p>当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#inputtype枚举说明">输入框的类型</a>设置为Password、NEW_PASSWORD和NUMBER_PASSWORD模式时，密码保护功能才能生效。非密码输入模式则不会触发该功能。</p>     <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#密码模式" target="_blank">密码模式</a>时，由于输入框后端的状态和前端应用侧的状态管理变量会不一致，可能导致末尾图标的状态异常。建议在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#onsecuritystatechange12">onSecurityStateChange</a>上增加状态同步。参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#示例1设置与获取光标位置">示例1（设置与获取光标位置）</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">visible</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否显示密码。</p>          <p>true表示会显示密码，false表示不会显示密码。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 589px;">     <h3 id="linebreakstrategy12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">lineBreakStrategy<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="linebreakstrategy12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>lineBreakStrategy(strategy: LineBreakStrategy)</p>     <p>设置折行规则。该属性在wordBreak不等于breakAll的时候生效，不支持连词符。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本的折行规则。</p>          <p>默认值：LineBreakStrategy.GREEDY</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>仅设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#内联模式" target="_blank">内联模式</a>时该属性生效。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 541px;">     <h3 id="editmenuoptions12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">editMenuOptions<sup>12+</sup><i <p>设置自定义菜单扩展项，允许用户设置扩展项的文本内容、图标、回调方法。</p>     <p>调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-textmenucontroller#disablesystemservicemenuitems20">disableSystemServiceMenuItems</a>接口屏蔽文本选择菜单内的系统服务菜单项时，editMenuOptions接口内回调方法<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#oncreatemenu12">onCreateMenu</a>的入参列表中不包含被屏蔽的菜单选项。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version id="enablepreviewtext12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enablePreviewText<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enablepreviewtext12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enablePreviewText(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否开启输入预上屏。</p>     <p>预上屏内容定义为文字暂存态，目前不支持文字拦截功能。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.55.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enable</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>是否开启输入预上屏。</p>          <p>true表示开启输入预上屏，false表示不开启输入预上屏。</p>          <p>默认值：true</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>“预上屏”描述的是一种文字暂存状态。需要在输入法中开启预上屏功能，在输入文本过程中，未确认输入候选词时，文本框中显示标记文本。例如，通过拼音输入中文时，未确定候选词之前，在输入框中显示拼音字母，该状态称为文字预上屏。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">InputType枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="inputtype枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.3.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.3.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.69.3.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Normal</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>基本输入模式，无特殊限制。</p>          <p>内联输入风格只支持InputType.Normal类型。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Password</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>密码输入模式。</p>          <p>默认输入文字短暂显示后变成圆点。从API version 12开始，PC/2in1设备上输入文字直接显示为圆点。</p>          <p>TV设备上输入框末尾默认不显示小眼睛图标，其他设备输入框末尾默认显示小眼睛图标。</p>          <p>密码输入模式中，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#decoration12">decoration</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#showunderline10">showUnderline</a>不生效。</p>          <p>在已启用密码保险箱的情况下，支持用户名、密码的自动保存和自动填充。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Email</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>邮箱地址输入模式。</p>          <p>支持数字、字母、下划线、小数点、!、#、$、%、&amp;、'、"、*、+、-、/、=、?、^、`、{、|、}、~，以及@字符（只能存在一个@字符）。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">Number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>纯数字输入模式。</p>          <p>不支持负数、小数。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">PhoneNumber<sup>9+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">-</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>电话号码输入模式。</p>          <p>支持输入数字、空格、+ 、-、*、#、(、)，长度不限。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NUMBER_PASSWORD<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">8</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>纯数字密码输入模式。</p>          <p>默认输入文字短暂显示后变成圆点。从API version 12开始，PC/2in1设备上输入文字直接显示为圆点。</p>          <p>TV设备上输入框末尾默认不显示小眼睛图标，其他设备输入框末尾默认显示小眼睛图标。</p>          <p>密码输入模式不支持下划线样式。在已启用密码保险箱的情况下，支持用户名、密码的自动保存和自动填充。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">USER_NAME<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">10</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>用户名输入模式，无特殊限制。</p>          <p>在已启用密码保险箱的情况下，支持用户名、密码的自动保存和自动填充。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NEW_PASSWORD<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">11</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" <p>在已启用密码保险箱的情况下，支持自动生成新密码。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NUMBER_DECIMAL<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">12</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">          <p>带小数点的数字输入模式。</p>          <p>支持数字，小数点（只能存在一个小数点）。不支持负数小数，负数小数的数字输入模式请使用inputFilter实现。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">URL<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">13</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Default</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">默认风格，光标宽1.5vp，光标高度与文本选中底板高度和字体大小相关。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Inline</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>内联输入风格。文本选中底板高度与输入框高度相同。</p>          <p>内联输入是在有明显的编辑态/非编辑态的区分场景下使用，例如：文件列表视图中的重命名。</p>          <p>不支持showError属性。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-common-components-text-input#内联模式" target="_blank">内联模式</a>下，不支持拖入文本。</p></td> class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="事件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 525px;">     <h3 id="onchange" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onChange<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onchange" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onChange(callback: EditableTextOnChangeCallback)</p>     <p>输入内容发生变化时，触发该回调。</p>     <p>在本回调中，若执行了光标操作，需要开发者在预上屏场景下依据previewText参数调整光标逻辑，以适应预上屏场景。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.75.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#editabletextonchangecallback12">EditableTextOnChangeCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 541px;">     <h3 id="onsubmit" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onSubmit<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onSubmit(callback: OnSubmitCallback)</p>     <p>按下输入法回车键触发该回调。</p>     <p>非TV设备按下回车键时输入框默认会失焦且收起键盘，可在OnSubmitCallback回调中配置是否收起键盘，参考<a <h3 id="oneditchange8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onEditChange<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i <p>设置文本选择区域并高亮显示。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.95.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left"  </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>如果selectionStart或selectionEnd被赋值为undefined时，当作0处理。</p>       <p>如果selectionMenuHidden被赋值为true或设备为2in1时，即使options被赋值为MenuPolicy.SHOW，调用setTextSelection也不弹出菜单。</p>       <p>如果emoji表情被选中区域截断时，表情的起始位置包含在设置的文本选中区域内就会被选中。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 318px;">     <h3 id="stopediting10" class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type OnSubmitCallback = (enterKey: EnterKeyType, event: SubmitEvent) =&gt; void</p>     <p>提交回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.102.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.102.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">enterKey</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" id="ontextselectionchangecallback18" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">OnTextSelectionChangeCallback<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.103.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th 10开始支持</span></li><li>      }</li><li>    }</li><li>    .<span class="hljs-title function_">width</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'100%'</span>)</li><li>    .<span class="hljs-title href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-textinput#wordbreak12">wordBreak</a>属性实现了TextInput不同断行规则下的效果。</p>     <div _ngcontent-vle-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-vle-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-vle-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-vle-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-comment">// xxx.ets</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Entry</span></li><li><span class="hljs-meta">@Component</span></li><li>struct <span class="hljs-title
